\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01154}01154\ def\ test\_class\_weights(name):}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01158}01158\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Iris\ is\ balanced,\ so\ no\ effect\ expected\ for\ using\ 'balanced'\ weights}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01159}01159\ \ \ \ \ clf1\ =\ TreeClassifier(random\_state=0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01160}01160\ \ \ \ \ clf1.fit(iris.data,\ iris.target)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01164}01164\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01165}01165\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Make\ a\ multi-\/output\ problem\ with\ three\ copies\ of\ Iris}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01166}01166\ \ \ \ \ iris\_multi\ =\ np.vstack((iris.target,\ iris.target,\ iris.target)).T}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01167}01167\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Create\ user-\/defined\ weights\ that\ should\ balance\ over\ the\ outputs}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01168}01168\ \ \ \ \ clf3\ =\ TreeClassifier(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01169}01169\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ class\_weight=[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01170}01170\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{0:\ 2.0,\ 1:\ 2.0,\ 2:\ 1.0\},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01171}01171\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{0:\ 2.0,\ 1:\ 1.0,\ 2:\ 2.0\},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01172}01172\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{0:\ 1.0,\ 1:\ 2.0,\ 2:\ 2.0\},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01173}01173\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01174}01174\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ random\_state=0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01175}01175\ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01176}01176\ \ \ \ \ clf3.fit(iris.data,\ iris\_multi)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01177}01177\ \ \ \ \ assert\_almost\_equal(clf2.feature\_importances\_,\ clf3.feature\_importances\_)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01178}01178\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Check\ against\ multi-\/output\ "{}auto"{}\ which\ should\ also\ have\ no\ effect}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01180}01180\ \ \ \ \ clf4.fit(iris.data,\ iris\_multi)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01182}01182\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01183}01183\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Inflate\ importance\ of\ class\ 1,\ check\ against\ user-\/defined\ weights}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01184}01184\ \ \ \ \ sample\_weight\ =\ np.ones(iris.target.shape)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01185}01185\ \ \ \ \ sample\_weight[iris.target\ ==\ 1]\ *=\ 100}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01186}01186\ \ \ \ \ class\_weight\ =\ \{0:\ 1.0,\ 1:\ 100.0,\ 2:\ 1.0\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01187}01187\ \ \ \ \ clf1\ =\ TreeClassifier(random\_state=0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01188}01188\ \ \ \ \ clf1.fit(iris.data,\ iris.target,\ sample\_weight)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01189}01189\ \ \ \ \ clf2\ =\ TreeClassifier(class\_weight=class\_weight,\ random\_state=0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01190}01190\ \ \ \ \ clf2.fit(iris.data,\ iris.target)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01191}01191\ \ \ \ \ assert\_almost\_equal(clf1.feature\_importances\_,\ clf2.feature\_importances\_)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01192}01192\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01193}01193\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Check\ that\ sample\_weight\ and\ class\_weight\ are\ multiplicative}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01492}01492\ \ \ \ \ data\ =\ []}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01493}01493\ \ \ \ \ offset\ =\ 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01494}01494\ \ \ \ \ indptr\ =\ [offset]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01495}01495\ \ \ \ \ for\ i\ in\ range(n\_features):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01496}01496\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\_nonzero\_i\ =\ random\_state.binomial(n\_samples,\ 0.5)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01497}01497\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ indices\_i\ =\ random\_state.permutation(samples)[:n\_nonzero\_i]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01498}01498\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ indices.append(indices\_i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01499}01499\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ data\_i\ =\ random\_state.binomial(3,\ 0.5,\ size=(n\_nonzero\_i,))\ -\/\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01500}01500\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ data.append(data\_i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01501}01501\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ offset\ +=\ n\_nonzero\_i}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01502}01502\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ indptr.append(offset)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01503}01503\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01504}01504\ \ \ \ \ indices\ =\ np.concatenate(indices).astype(np.int32)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01505}01505\ \ \ \ \ indptr\ =\ np.array(indptr,\ dtype=np.int32)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01506}01506\ \ \ \ \ data\ =\ np.array(np.concatenate(data),\ dtype=np.float32)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01678}01678\ \ \ \ \ Because\ we\ are\ dealing\ with\ sample\ weights,\ we\ cannot\ find\ the\ median\ by}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01679}01679\ \ \ \ \ simply\ choosing/averaging\ the\ centre\ value(s),\ instead\ we\ consider\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01680}01680\ \ \ \ \ median\ where\ 50\%\ of\ the\ cumulative\ weight\ is\ found\ (in\ a\ y\ sorted\ data\ set)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01681}01681\ \ \ \ \ .\ Therefore\ with\ regards\ to\ this\ test\ data,\ the\ cumulative\ weight\ is\ >=\ 50\%}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01682}01682\ \ \ \ \ when\ y\ =\ 4.\ \ Therefore:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01683}01683\ \ \ \ \ Median\ =\ 4}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01684}01684\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01685}01685\ \ \ \ \ For\ all\ the\ samples,\ we\ can\ get\ the\ total\ error\ by\ summing:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01686}01686\ \ \ \ \ Absolute(Median\ -\/\ y)\ *\ weight}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01687}01687\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01688}01688\ \ \ \ \ I.e.,\ total\ error\ =\ (Absolute(4\ -\/\ 3)\ *\ 0.1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01689}01689\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ +\ (Absolute(4\ -\/\ 3)\ *\ 0.3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01690}01690\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ +\ (Absolute(4\ -\/\ 4)\ *\ 1.0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01691}01691\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ +\ (Absolute(4\ -\/\ 6)\ *\ 0.6)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01692}01692\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ +\ (Absolute(4\ -\/\ 7)\ *\ 0.3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01693}01693\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 2.5}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01694}01694\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01725}01725\ \ \ \ \ Likewise\ for\ Right\ node:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01726}01726\ \ \ \ \ Right\ node\ Median\ =\ 4}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01727}01727\ \ \ \ \ Total\ error\ =\ (Absolute(4\ -\/\ 3)\ *\ 0.3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01728}01728\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ +\ (Absolute(4\ -\/\ 4)\ *\ 1.0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01729}01729\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ +\ (Absolute(4\ -\/\ 7)\ *\ 0.3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01730}01730\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1.2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01731}01731\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01732}01732\ \ \ \ \ Right\ Impurity\ =\ Total\ error\ /\ total\ weight}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01733}01733\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1.2\ /\ 1.6}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01734}01734\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 0.75}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01735}01735\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01736}01736\ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}"{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01793}01793\ \ \ \ \ \#\ try\ to\ make\ empty\ leaf\ by\ using\ near\ infinite\ value.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01796}01796\ \ \ \ \ X\ =\ data[:,\ :-\/1]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01797}01797\ \ \ \ \ if\ sparse\_container\ is\ not\ None:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01801}01801\ \ \ \ \ tree\ =\ DecisionTreeRegressor(random\_state=0).fit(X,\ y)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01874}01874\ \ \ \ \ assert\ tree.max\_depth\ >=\ subtree.max\_depth}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01875}01875\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01876}01876\ \ \ \ \ tree\_c\_left\ =\ tree.children\_left}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01882}01882\ \ \ \ \ while\ stack:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01883}01883\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ tree\_node\_idx,\ subtree\_node\_idx\ =\ stack.pop()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01884}01884\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ assert\_array\_almost\_equal(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01885}01885\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ tree.value[tree\_node\_idx],\ subtree.value[subtree\_node\_idx]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01886}01886\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01889}01889\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01892}01892\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01893}01893\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ assert\_almost\_equal(}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01895}01895\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ subtree.weighted\_n\_node\_samples[subtree\_node\_idx],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01896}01896\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01897}01897\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01898}01898\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ subtree\_c\_left[subtree\_node\_idx]\ ==\ subtree\_c\_right[subtree\_node\_idx]:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01899}01899\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ is\ a\ leaf}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01900}01900\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ assert\_almost\_equal(TREE\_UNDEFINED,\ subtree.threshold[subtree\_node\_idx])}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01901}01901\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ else:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01943}01943\ def\ test\_balance\_property(criterion,\ Tree):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01944}01944\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Test\ that\ sum(y\_pred)=sum(y\_true)\ on\ training\ set.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01945}01945\ \ \ \ \ \#\ This\ works\ if\ the\ mean\ is\ predicted\ (should\ even\ be\ true\ for\ each\ leaf).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01946}01946\ \ \ \ \ \#\ MAE\ predicts\ the\ median\ and\ is\ therefore\ excluded\ from\ this\ test.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01947}01947\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01948}01948\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Choose\ a\ training\ set\ with\ non-\/negative\ targets\ (for\ poisson)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01949}01949\ \ \ \ \ X,\ y\ =\ diabetes.data,\ diabetes.target}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01950}01950\ \ \ \ \ reg\ =\ Tree(criterion=criterion)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01951}01951\ \ \ \ \ reg.fit(X,\ y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01952}01952\ \ \ \ \ assert\ np.sum(reg.predict(X))\ ==\ pytest.approx(np.sum(y))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01953}01953\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01954}01954\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01955}01955\ @pytest.mark.parametrize("{}seed"{},\ range(3))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01956}01956\ def\ test\_poisson\_zero\_nodes(seed):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01957}01957\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Test\ that\ sum(y)=0\ and\ therefore\ y\_pred=0\ is\ forbidden\ on\ nodes.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01958}01958\ \ \ \ \ X\ =\ [[0,\ 0],\ [0,\ 1],\ [0,\ 2],\ [0,\ 3],\ [1,\ 0],\ [1,\ 2],\ [1,\ 2],\ [1,\ 3]]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01959}01959\ \ \ \ \ y\ =\ [0,\ 0,\ 0,\ 0,\ 1,\ 2,\ 3,\ 4]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01960}01960\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Note\ that\ X[:,\ 0]\ ==\ 0\ is\ a\ 100\%\ indicator\ for\ y\ ==\ 0.\ The\ tree\ can}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01961}01961\ \ \ \ \ \#\ easily\ learn\ that:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01962}01962\ \ \ \ \ reg\ =\ DecisionTreeRegressor(criterion="{}squared\_error"{},\ random\_state=seed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01963}01963\ \ \ \ \ reg.fit(X,\ y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01964}01964\ \ \ \ \ assert\ np.amin(reg.predict(X))\ ==\ 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01965}01965\ \ \ \ \ \#\ whereas\ Poisson\ must\ predict\ strictly\ positive\ numbers}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01966}01966\ \ \ \ \ reg\ =\ DecisionTreeRegressor(criterion="{}poisson"{},\ random\_state=seed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01967}01967\ \ \ \ \ reg.fit(X,\ y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01968}01968\ \ \ \ \ assert\ np.all(reg.predict(X)\ >\ 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01969}01969\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01970}01970\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Test\ additional\ dataset\ where\ something\ could\ go\ wrong.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01971}01971\ \ \ \ \ n\_features\ =\ 10}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01972}01972\ \ \ \ \ X,\ y\ =\ datasets.make\_regression(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01973}01973\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ effective\_rank=n\_features\ *\ 2\ //\ 3,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01974}01974\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ tail\_strength=0.6,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01975}01975\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\_samples=1\_000,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01976}01976\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\_features=n\_features,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01977}01977\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\_informative=n\_features\ *\ 2\ //\ 3,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01978}01978\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ random\_state=seed,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01979}01979\ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01980}01980\ \ \ \ \ \#\ some\ excess\ zeros}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01981}01981\ \ \ \ \ y[(-\/1\ <\ y)\ \&\ (y\ <\ 0)]\ =\ 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01982}01982\ \ \ \ \ \#\ make\ sure\ the\ target\ is\ positive}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01983}01983\ \ \ \ \ y\ =\ np.abs(y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01984}01984\ \ \ \ \ reg\ =\ DecisionTreeRegressor(criterion="{}poisson"{},\ random\_state=seed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01985}01985\ \ \ \ \ reg.fit(X,\ y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01986}01986\ \ \ \ \ assert\ np.all(reg.predict(X)\ >\ 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01987}01987\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01988}01988\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01989}01989\ def\ test\_poisson\_vs\_mse():}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01990}01990\ \ \ \ \ \#\ For\ a\ Poisson\ distributed\ target,\ Poisson\ loss\ should\ give\ better\ results}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01991}01991\ \ \ \ \ \#\ than\ squared\ error\ measured\ in\ Poisson\ deviance\ as\ metric.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01992}01992\ \ \ \ \ \#\ We\ have\ a\ similar\ test,\ test\_poisson(),\ in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01993}01993\ \ \ \ \ \#\ sklearn/ensemble/\_hist\_gradient\_boosting/tests/test\_gradient\_boosting.py}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01994}01994\ \ \ \ \ rng\ =\ np.random.RandomState(42)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01995}01995\ \ \ \ \ n\_train,\ n\_test,\ n\_features\ =\ 500,\ 500,\ 10}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01996}01996\ \ \ \ \ X\ =\ datasets.make\_low\_rank\_matrix(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01997}01997\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\_samples=n\_train\ +\ n\_test,\ n\_features=n\_features,\ random\_state=rng}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01998}01998\ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l01999}01999\ \ \ \ \ \#\ We\ create\ a\ log-\/linear\ Poisson\ model\ and\ downscale\ coef\ as\ it\ will\ get}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02000}02000\ \ \ \ \ \#\ exponentiated.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02001}02001\ \ \ \ \ coef\ =\ rng.uniform(low=-\/2,\ high=2,\ size=n\_features)\ /\ np.max(X,\ axis=0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02002}02002\ \ \ \ \ y\ =\ rng.poisson(lam=np.exp(X\ @\ coef))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02003}02003\ \ \ \ \ X\_train,\ X\_test,\ y\_train,\ y\_test\ =\ train\_test\_split(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02004}02004\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ X,\ y,\ test\_size=n\_test,\ random\_state=rng}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02005}02005\ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02006}02006\ \ \ \ \ \#\ We\ prevent\ some\ overfitting\ by\ setting\ min\_samples\_split=10.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02007}02007\ \ \ \ \ tree\_poi\ =\ DecisionTreeRegressor(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02008}02008\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ criterion="{}poisson"{},\ min\_samples\_split=10,\ random\_state=rng}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02009}02009\ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02010}02010\ \ \ \ \ tree\_mse\ =\ DecisionTreeRegressor(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02011}02011\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ criterion="{}squared\_error"{},\ min\_samples\_split=10,\ random\_state=rng}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02012}02012\ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02013}02013\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02014}02014\ \ \ \ \ tree\_poi.fit(X\_train,\ y\_train)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02015}02015\ \ \ \ \ tree\_mse.fit(X\_train,\ y\_train)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02016}02016\ \ \ \ \ dummy\ =\ DummyRegressor(strategy="{}mean"{}).fit(X\_train,\ y\_train)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02017}02017\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02018}02018\ \ \ \ \ for\ X,\ y,\ val\ in\ [(X\_train,\ y\_train,\ "{}train"{}),\ (X\_test,\ y\_test,\ "{}test"{})]:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02019}02019\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ metric\_poi\ =\ mean\_poisson\_deviance(y,\ tree\_poi.predict(X))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02020}02020\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ squared\_error\ might\ produce\ non-\/positive\ predictions\ =>\ clip}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02021}02021\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ metric\_mse\ =\ mean\_poisson\_deviance(y,\ np.clip(tree\_mse.predict(X),\ 1e-\/15,\ None))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02022}02022\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ metric\_dummy\ =\ mean\_poisson\_deviance(y,\ dummy.predict(X))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02023}02023\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ As\ squared\_error\ might\ correctly\ predict\ 0\ in\ train\ set,\ its\ train}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02024}02024\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ score\ can\ be\ better\ than\ Poisson.\ This\ is\ no\ longer\ the\ case\ for\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02025}02025\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ test\ set.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02026}02026\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ val\ ==\ "{}test"{}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02027}02027\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ assert\ metric\_poi\ <\ 0.5\ *\ metric\_mse}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02028}02028\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ assert\ metric\_poi\ <\ 0.75\ *\ metric\_dummy}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02029}02029\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__tree_8py_source_l02030}02030\ }
